   <h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading">Spam blacklist/Log</h1> 
   <div id="bodyContent" class="vector-body"> 
    <div id="siteSub" class="noprint">
     From Meta, a Wikimedia project coordination wiki
    </div> 
    <div id="contentSub">
     <span class="subpages">&lt; <a href="/wiki/Spam_blacklist" title="Spam blacklist">Spam blacklist</a></span>
    </div> 
    <div id="contentSub2"></div> 
    <div id="jump-to-nav"></div> <a class="mw-jump-link" href="#mw-head">Jump to navigation</a> <a class="mw-jump-link" href="#searchInput">Jump to search</a>

     <div class="mw-parser-output">
      <table style="width: 100%; border: 1px solid #060; background: #dfd; margin-top: 2px; margin-bottom: 2px;"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr> 
         <td style="width: 20%; text-align: left; font-size: 90%">?<a href="/wiki/Talk:Spam_blacklist" title="Talk:Spam blacklist">Talk:Spam blacklist</a> </td> 
         <td style="text-align: center"><b><a href="/wiki/Spam_blacklist" title="Spam blacklist">Spam blacklist</a></b> (log) </td> 
         <td style="width: 20%; text-align: right; font-size: 90%"> </td>
        </tr>
       </tbody>
      </table> 
      <table style="width:100%; border:1px solid grey; background:#fafaff; margin:1ex 0"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr> 
         <td> This is the entry log for the <a href="/wiki/Spam_blacklist" title="Spam blacklist">Spam blacklist</a>; all additions should be logged so that future users can easily find the reason. You can make a single row for multiple entries, assuming the same reason applies to all of them. If you remove something from the blacklist, simply remove the relevant entry here.</td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table>

      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Search">Search</span></h2> 
      <div class="mw-inputbox-centered" style="">
       <form name="searchbox" class="searchbox" action="/wiki/Special:Search">
        <input class="mw-inputbox-input mw-searchInput searchboxInput mw-ui-input mw-ui-input-inline" name="search" type="text" value="" placeholder="" size="50" dir="ltr">
        <input type="hidden" value="Spam blacklist/Log" name="prefix">
        <br>
        <input type="submit" name="fulltext" class="mw-ui-button" value="Search in this page hierarchy">
        <input type="hidden" value="Search" name="fulltext">
       </form>
      </div> 
      <dl>
       <dt>
        Hint
       </dt> 
       <dd>
        If you are searching for a specific incidence you should also trying adding a leading <b>b</b> to your search term. This will account for the regular expression component used. 
        <ul>
         <li>example: search <code class="mw-highlight mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr">bdirectory</code> rather than <code class="mw-highlight mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr">directory</code></li>
        </ul>
       </dd>
      </dl> 
      <p><br> </p> 
      <div class="center" style="width:auto; margin-left:auto; margin-right:auto;">
       <b>See <a href="/wiki/Spam_blacklist/Log/Archive" title="Spam blacklist/Log/Archive">Archive</a> for entries before 2020.</b>
      </div> 
      <p><br> </p> 
      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Documentation">Documentation</span></h2> 
      <div style="border: 1px solid gray; border-radius: 3px; margin: 0px 0px 0pt 0pt; padding: 0em 1em 1em;"> 
       <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adding_entries">Adding entries</span></h3> 
       <p>Please use <i>exactly</i> the following format. The log file is read by machines. So please don't use comments like "see above" or "see following entry". </p> 
       <h4><span class="mw-headline" id="For_requests_on_Talk:Spam_blacklist">For requests on <a href="/wiki/Talk:Spam_blacklist" title="Talk:Spam blacklist">Talk:Spam blacklist</a></span></h4> 
       <ol>
        <li>Take the logging snippets from both <a href="/wiki/Talk:Spam_blacklist" title="Talk:Spam blacklist">Talk:Spam blacklist</a> and <a href="/wiki/Spam_blacklist" title="Spam blacklist">Spam blacklist</a> after your edits. (Mark the request as done, then take the logging <a href="/wiki/Talk:Spam_blacklist#oldid" title="Talk:Spam blacklist">snippet</a> provided there; add your regex(es) to the blacklist and then take the <a href="/wiki/Spam_blacklist#oldid" title="Spam blacklist">snippet</a> there.) 
         <ul>
          <li>For additions, use <span style="color:green;">{{sbl-diff|1161261}}; see {{sbl-log|1161258#{{subst:anchorencode:Example}}}}</span>, which produces <span class="plainlinks"><a class="external text" href="https://meta.wikimedia.org/w/index.php?title=Spam_blacklist&amp;diff=prev&amp;oldid=1161261&amp;diffonly=yes">addition</a></span>; see <span class="plainlinks"><a class="external text" href="https://meta.wikimedia.org/w/index.php?title=Talk:Spam_blacklist&amp;oldid=1161258#Example">request</a></span></li> 
          <li>For removals, use <span style="color:red;">{{sbl-diff|1161261|removal}}; see {{sbl-log|1161258#{{subst:anchorencode:Example}}}}</span>, which produces <span class="plainlinks"><a class="external text" href="https://meta.wikimedia.org/w/index.php?title=Spam_blacklist&amp;diff=prev&amp;oldid=1161261&amp;diffonly=yes">removal</a></span>; see <span class="plainlinks"><a class="external text" href="https://meta.wikimedia.org/w/index.php?title=Talk:Spam_blacklist&amp;oldid=1161258#Example">request</a></span></li> 
          <li>For changes, use <span style="color:blue;">{{sbl-diff|1161261|change}}; see {{sbl-log|1161258#{{subst:anchorencode:Example}}}}</span>, which produces <span class="plainlinks"><a class="external text" href="https://meta.wikimedia.org/w/index.php?title=Spam_blacklist&amp;diff=prev&amp;oldid=1161261&amp;diffonly=yes">change</a></span>; see <span class="plainlinks"><a class="external text" href="https://meta.wikimedia.org/w/index.php?title=Talk:Spam_blacklist&amp;oldid=1161258#Example">request</a></span></li>
         </ul></li> 
        <li>For single entries, write the entry and log data on the same line.</li> 
        <li>For multiple entries, put the log data on a line beginning with " #:", then list the entries on new lines below indented by three spaces to set the regexes apart.</li>
       </ol> 
       <h4><span class="mw-headline" id="For_bot_reports">For <a href="/wiki/User:COIBot/XWiki" title="User:COIBot/XWiki">bot reports</a></span></h4> 
       <ul>
        <li>The log entry is provided to you; simply complete the <code>{{<a href="/wiki/Template:Sbl-diff" title="Template:Sbl-diff">sbl-diff</a>|#}}</code>, using <a href="/wiki/Spam_blacklist#oldid" title="Spam blacklist">the number</a> taken after your edit to the blacklist.</li> 
        <li>Put your username in place of ADMINNAME unless you use "<a href="/wiki/User:Mike.lifeguard/coibot.js" title="User:Mike.lifeguard/coibot.js">COIBot log tool</a>".</li> 
        <li>If you use "SBHandler" (on the <i>Gadgets</i> tab of <a href="/wiki/Special:Preferences" title="Special:Preferences"><i>my preferences</i></a> then this is all done for you)</li>
       </ul> 
       <table class="mw-collapsible mw-collapsed" style="margin: 2px 0; background: #FFF; color: #000; width: 100%; border: 1px solid #AAA; padding: 0; border-spacing: 0; border-collapse: collapse;"> 
        <tbody>
         <tr> 
          <th style="padding: 2px;">
           <div style="background:#CCF;padding:2px 0.5em;font-weight:bold;text-align:center;">
            Example:
           </div> </th>
         </tr> 
         <tr> 
          <td style="padding: 2px; background:transparent;font-weight:normal;text-align:left;"> 
           <dl>
            <dd></dd>
           </dl> <pre>entry                          # Admin          # log data
----------------------------------------------------------
spam\.com                      # Mike.lifeguard # <span class="plainlinks"><a class="external text" href="https://meta.wikimedia.org/w/index.php?title=Spam_blacklist&amp;diff=prev&amp;oldid=1161240&amp;diffonly=yes">addition</a></span>; see <a href="/wiki/User:COIBot/XWiki/spam.com" class="mw-redirect" title="User:COIBot/XWiki/spam.com">User:COIBot/XWiki/spam.com</a>
#:                             # A.B.           # <span class="plainlinks"><a class="external text" href="https://meta.wikimedia.org/w/index.php?title=Spam_blacklist&amp;diff=prev&amp;oldid=1161242&amp;diffonly=yes">addition</a></span>; see <span class="plainlinks"><a class="external text" href="https://meta.wikimedia.org/w/index.php?title=Talk:Spam_blacklist&amp;oldid=1161253#silliness">request</a></span>
  \buuf\.com\b
  \bufu\.com\b
  \bexample\.com\b
  \b[fu]{3}\.ca\b
\buuf\.com\b                   # Herbythyme     # <span class="plainlinks"><a class="external text" href="https://meta.wikimedia.org/w/index.php?title=Spam_blacklist&amp;diff=prev&amp;oldid=10987&amp;diffonly=yes">removal</a></span>; see <span class="plainlinks"><a class="external text" href="https://meta.wikimedia.org/w/index.php?title=Talk:Spam_blacklist&amp;oldid=12345#uuf.com">request</a></span>
spam\.com ? \bspam\.com\b      # Beetstra       # <span class="plainlinks"><a class="external text" href="https://meta.wikimedia.org/w/index.php?title=Spam_blacklist&amp;diff=prev&amp;oldid=1161241&amp;diffonly=yes">change</a></span>; see <span class="plainlinks"><a class="external text" href="https://meta.wikimedia.org/w/index.php?title=Talk:Spam_blacklist&amp;oldid=1161252#mistake">request</a></span>

         </tr>

       </table>
